name:b‚Äça‚Äçm‚Äçb‚Äço‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:27 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted February 17, 2024
msg:Eight years ago, a friend introduced me to this treasure resort hotel. At that time, the owner was still Shanghai Greenland. The use of Greenland Platinum luxury brand was enough to show the owner's investment and positioning in this project. However, not long after, the owner resold the hotel to Hangzhou local owner Xintiandi and renamed it Pu Shi brand. Despite this, the excellent features of the hotel have been preserved. All 82 guest rooms are designed with Hui-style courtyards, which are integrated with the local culture at the junction of Zhejiang and Anhui in the Xin'an River Basin. Each guest room has its own characteristic vegetation in the courtyard.
The housekeeper took it to the door of the mansion, and the lantern with the owner's surname üèÆ restored the culture of the wealthy residences in Wenyuan Lion City to the extreme, and the stay experience was instantly enhanced.
The Hui-style courtyard of Xin'an Garden, where I stayed this time, adopts a three-entry design. The first entrance uses a traditional key to open the door to see the outdoor courtyard. The second entrance is the indoor living hall, and the third entrance is the second-floor bedroom. The traditional wooden house style design instantly brings an immersive Jiangnan vacation experience. The bathroom is large and equipped with a double basin design and a deep soaking bathtub. At a time when cost control of toiletries is popular, it is still adhering to the original intention of using more hygienic small bottles. You can enjoy the hotel's fitness facilities, tour the replica of the ancient city and perform all day. If it weren't for the lack of privacy in the ancient city, it would be a substitute for Amman or Ritz-Carlton Hidden Resort, but the room rate may be only 10% of theirs, how high is the cost performance. In terms of service, three of us checked in, and the front desk took the initiative to arrange for the delivery of quilts and toiletries. They greeted us with a smile throughout the whole process and guided us to introduce the hotel facilities and how to use them. It was very professional. The only two weaknesses are that the quality of the hotel's catering has a lot of room for improvement. During the New Year, the Chinese restaurant only has set meals available and the price of the dishes has increased a lot. The quality of the breakfast ingredients in the buffet restaurant is too low, which is not in line with the hotel's positioning. The swimming pool is open too late, and I hope it will be improved.
